&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;Vim被誉为编辑器之神，是程序员为程序员设计的编辑器，编辑效率高，十分适合编辑代码，其界面如下图所示。对于习惯了图形化界面文本编辑软件的同学们来说，刚接触Vim时一定会觉得非常不习惯非常不顺手，所以在这里给大家总结了一些常用的基本操作以助入门。同时，推荐给大家一篇质量极高的Vim教程&mdash;&mdash;《简明Vim练级攻略》(<a href="http://coolshell.cn/articles/5426.html/" class="uri">http://coolshell.cn/articles/5426.html/</a>)，只需要十多分钟的阅读，你就可以掌握 Vim的所有基本操作。当然，想要完全掌握它需要相当长的时间去练习，而如果你只想把Vim当成记事本用的话，几分钟的学习足矣。其他的内容网上有太多太多的资料，随用随查即可。</p> <div class="figure" style="padding-left: 30px;"><img src="/assets/courseware/v1/afe694b341256815756f672c8e024ebe/asset-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@asset+block/0-21_-_%E6%94%B9.jpg" alt="Vim界面及基础介绍" type="saveimage" target="[object Object]" width="833" height="618" /> <p class="caption" style="padding-left: 330px;">Vim界面及基础介绍<span data-label="fig:0-21"></span></p> </div> <p></p> </div> </div> <div class="vert vert-1" data-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@discussion+block@ba8d1831ba564fa7b07a3c12b3b08628"> <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-discussion" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="DiscussionInlineBlock" data-course-id="course-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2" data-request-token="8599ab26546f11ea990c5254001c17d8" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@discussion+block@ba8d1831ba564fa7b07a3c12b3b08628" data-block-type="discussion"> <script type="text/javascript"> window.PLATFORM_NAME = "CSCore"; <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-vertical" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="VerticalStudentView" data-course-id="course-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2" data-request-token="8599ab26546f11ea990c5254001c17d8" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@vertical+block@03cb10b4bae142ebb79ba4ed307eb669" data-block-type="vertical"> <h3 class="unit-title">GCC</h3> <div class="bookmark-button-wrapper"> <button class="btn btn-link bookmark-button " aria-pressed="false" data-bookmark-id="18231047,block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@vertical+block@03cb10b4bae142ebb79ba4ed307eb669"> <span class="sr bookmark-sr">Click to add</span> <span class="bookmark-text">Bookmark this page</span> </button> </div> <div class="vert-mod"> <div class="vert vert-0" data-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@html+block@1cefdb76eb184dd6b5b9433d9e7d77e5"> <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-html xmodule_display xmodule_HtmlModule" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="XBlockToXModuleShim" data-block-type="html" data-request-token="8599ab26546f11ea990c5254001c17d8" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@html+block@1cefdb76eb184dd6b5b9433d9e7d77e5" data-type="HTMLModule" data-course-id="course-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2"> <script type="json/xblock-args" class="xblock-json-init-args"> {"xmodule-type": "HTMLModule"} </script> <p>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;在没有IDE的情况下，使用GCC编译器是一种简单快捷生成可执行文件的途径，只需一行命令即可将C源文件编译成可执行文件。其常用的使用方法如下所示，同学们可以自己动手实践，写一些简单的C代码来编译运行。如果想要同时编译多个文件，可以直接用-o选项将多个文件进行编译连接：gcc testfun.c test.c -o test ，也可以先使用-c选项将每个文件单独编译成.o文件，再用-o选项将多个.o文件进行连接：gcc -c testfun.c -&gt; gcc -c test.c -&gt; gcc testfun.o test.o -o test ，两者等价。</p> <div class="sourceCode" linenos=""> <pre class="sourceCode bash" style="padding-left: 90px;"><code class="sourceCode bash">语法:<span class="kw">gcc</span> [选项]... [参数]... 选项（常用）： <span class="kw">-o</span> 指定生成的输出文件 <span class="kw">-S</span> 将C代码转换为汇编代码 <span class="kw">-wall</span> 显示警告信息 <span class="kw">-c</span> 仅执行编译操作，不进行链接操作 <span class="kw">-M</span> 列出依赖<br /> -include filename 编译时用来包含头文件，功能相当于在代码中使用#include&lt;filename&gt;<br /> -Ipath 编译时指定头文件目录，使用标准库时不需要指定目录，</code>-I参数可以用相对路径，比如头文件在当前目录，可以用-I.来指定 <br /><br /></pre> <pre class="sourceCode bash" style="padding-left: 90px;"><code class="sourceCode bash">参数： <span class="kw">C</span>源文件：指定C语言源代码文件 <span class="kw">e.g.</span> $ <span class="kw">gcc</span> test.c <span class="co">#默认生成名为a.out的可执行文件</span> <span class="co">#Windows平台为a.exe</span> $ <span class="kw">gcc</span> test.c -o test <span class="co">#使用-o选项生成名为test的可执行文件</span> <span class="co">#Windows平台为test.exe</span></code></pre> </div> <p></p> </div> </div> <div class="vert vert-1" data-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@discussion+block@4988b6269c7e4af5bd35176dce3eb0ec"> <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-discussion" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="DiscussionInlineBlock" data-course-id="course-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2" data-request-token="8599ab26546f11ea990c5254001c17d8" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@discussion+block@4988b6269c7e4af5bd35176dce3eb0ec" data-block-type="discussion"> <script type="text/javascript"> window.PLATFORM_NAME = "CSCore"; window.ENABLE_DISCUSSION_HOME_PANEL = true; </script> <script aria-hidden="true" type="text/template" id="thread-template"> <article class="discussion-article" data-id="<%- id %>" tabindex="-1"> <div class="thread-wrapper"> <div class="thread-main-wrapper"> <div class="thread-content-wrapper"></div> <div class="post-extended-content"> <ol class="responses js-marked-answer-list"></ol> </div> </div> <div class="post-extended-content thread-responses-wrapper"> <div class="response-btn-count-wrapper"> <% if (!readOnly) { %> <div class="add-response"> <button class="btn btn-small add-response-btn"> <%- gettext("Add a Response") %> </button> </div> <% } %> <div class="response-count"></div> </div> <ol class="responses js-response-list"></ol> <div class="response-pagination"></div> <div class="post-status-closed bottom-post-status" style="display: none"> <%- gettext("This thread is closed.") %> </div> <% if (can_create_comment && !readOnly) { %> <form class="discussion-reply-new" data-id="<%- id %>"> <h4><%- gettext("Add a response:") %></h4> <ul class="discussion-errors"></ul> <div class="reply-body" data-id="<%- id %>"></div> <div class="reply-post-control"> <button class="btn discussion-submit-post control-button"><%- gettext("Submit") %></button> </div> </form> <% } %> </div> </div> </article> </script> <script aria-hidden="true" type="text/template" id="thread-show-template"> <div class="discussion-post"> <header class="post-header"> <% if (!readOnly) { %> <div class="post-header-actions"> <%= _.template( $('#forum-actions').html())( { contentId: cid, contentType: 'post', primaryActions: ['vote', 'follow'], secondaryActions: ['pin', 'edit', 'delete', 'report', 'close'], readOnly: readOnly } ) %> </div> <% } %> <div class="post-header-content"> <h4 class="post-title"><%- title %></h4> <p class="posted-details"> <% var timeAgoHtml = interpolate( '<span class="timeago" title="%(created_at)s">%(created_at)s</span>', {created_at: created_at}, true ); <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-vertical" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="VerticalStudentView" data-course-id="course-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2" data-request-token="8599ab26546f11ea990c5254001c17d8" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@vertical+block@baf00bab961f44158af6f22533186a2e" data-block-type="vertical"> <h3 class="unit-title">进程与fork</h3> <div class="bookmark-button-wrapper"> <button class="btn btn-link bookmark-button " aria-pressed="false" data-bookmark-id="18231047,block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@vertical+block@baf00bab961f44158af6f22533186a2e"> <span class="sr bookmark-sr">Click to add</span> <span class="bookmark-text">Bookmark this page</span> </button> </div> <div class="vert-mod"> <div class="vert vert-0" data-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@html+block@e9161bdc46d945ca94eddcf292636563"> <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-html xmodule_display xmodule_HtmlModule" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="XBlockToXModuleShim" data-block-type="html" data-request-token="8599ab26546f11ea990c5254001c17d8" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@html+block@e9161bdc46d945ca94eddcf292636563" data-type="HTMLModule" data-course-id="course-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2"> <script type="json/xblock-args" class="xblock-json-init-args"> {"xmodule-type": "HTMLModule"} </script> <p class="MsoNormal">在该部分，同学们只需初步了解进程概念、认识<span lang="EN-US">fork</span>函数的效果即可，后续课程会对这两个概念进行进一步的讲解。</p> <p class="MsoNormal">进程：<span style="color: #333333; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">进程（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; color: #333333; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">Process</span><span style="color: #333333; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">）是计算机中的程序关于某数据集合上的一次运行活动，是系统进行资源分配和调度的基本单位，是操作系统结构的基础。<strong>狭义的说，</strong><b>进程就是正在运行程序的实例，是程序的一次执行</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; color: #333333; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">Fork</span>：直观<span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">意象是叉子的意思。在我们这里更像是分叉的意思，就好像一条河流动着，遇到一个分叉口，分成两条河一样，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">fork </span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">就是那个分叉口。在操作系统中，某个进程调用</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">fork() </span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">之后，将会以此为分叉分成两个进程运行。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">接下来我们通过一个例子直观感受</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">fork()</span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">函数的运行效果</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">int main(void){</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; int var;</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; pid_t pid;</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; printf("Before fork.\n");</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; pid = fork();</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; printf("After fork.\n");</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; if (pid == 0){</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; printf("this is son.\n");</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; } else {</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; printf("this is father.\n");</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, initial;">为进程编号数据类型，本质上为宏定义的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">unsigned int</span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">类型）</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">这段代码的输出结果：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 21.0pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">Before fork.</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">After fork.</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"> <br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">this is son.</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"> <br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">After fork.</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;"><br /> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Courier New'; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">this is father.</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">Fork()</span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">函数执行后，进程一分为二，出现了父子进程，父子进程会将</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">fork()</span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">函数后的代码均执行一遍，唯一的区别是，在子进程中，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">fork()</span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">函数的返回值为</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">0</span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">，在父进程中</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">fork()</span><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">函数的返回值为父进程的进程编号。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">函数的效果。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-vertical" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="VerticalStudentView" data-course-id="course-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2" data-request-token="8599ab26546f11ea990c5254001c17d8" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@vertical+block@9c11c1149a944bb18298ab8686c53f88" data-block-type="vertical"> <h3 class="unit-title">Makefile</h3> <div class="bookmark-button-wrapper"> <button class="btn btn-link bookmark-button " aria-pressed="false" data-bookmark-id="18231047,block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@vertical+block@9c11c1149a944bb18298ab8686c53f88"> <span class="sr bookmark-sr">Click to add</span> <span class="bookmark-text">Bookmark this page</span> </button> </div> <div class="vert-mod"> <div class="vert vert-0" data-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@html+block@2df238dcd8c24b69a3b16126c5bb834d"> <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-html xmodule_display xmodule_HtmlModule" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="XBlockToXModuleShim" data-block-type="html" data-request-token="8599ab26546f11ea990c5254001c17d8" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2+type@html+block@2df238dcd8c24b69a3b16126c5bb834d" data-type="HTMLModule" data-course-id="course-v1:Internal+B3I062140+2019_T2"> <script type="json/xblock-args" class="xblock-json-init-args"> {"xmodule-type": "HTMLModule"} </script> <p class="MsoNormal">当我们想要翻开代码大干一番的时候，却面临着一个天大的问题：这堆代码应当从何读起？答曰：<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>。当你不知所措的时候， 从<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>开始往往会是一个不错的选择。这时，有同学要问了：什么是<span lang="EN-US">make</span>？什么又是<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>呢？<span lang="EN-US"> make</span>工具一般用于维护工程。它可以根据时间戳自动判断项目的哪些部分是需要重新编译的，每次只重编译必要的部分。<span lang="EN-US">make</span>工具会读取<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>文件， 并根据<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>的内容来执行相应的编译操作。<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>类似于大家以前接触过的<span lang="EN-US">VC</span>工程文件。只不过不像<span lang="EN-US">VC</span>那样有图形界面，而是直接用类似脚本的方式实现的。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal">相较于<span lang="EN-US">VC</span>工程而言，<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>具有更高的灵活性（当然，高灵活性的代价就是学习成本会有所提升，这是必然的），可以方便地管理大型的项目。 而且<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>理论上支持任意的语言，只要其编译器可以通过<span lang="EN-US">shell</span>命令来调用。当你的项目可能会混合多种语言，有着复杂的构建流程的时候，<span lang="EN-US"> Makefile</span>便能展现出它真正的威力来。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal">为了使你更为清晰地了解<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>的基本概念，我们来写一个简单的<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>。假设我们手头有一个<span lang="EN-US">Hello World</span>程序需要编译。我们来为它写一个简易的<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>。 让我们从头开始，如果我们没有<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>，直接动手编译这个程序，我们需要下面这样一个指令<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"># </span>直接使用<span lang="EN-US">gcc</span>编译<span lang="EN-US">Hello World</span>程序<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">$ gcc -o hello_world hello_world.c<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal">那么，如果我们想把它写成<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>，我们应该怎么办呢？<span lang="EN-US">makefile</span>最基本的格式是这样的<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">target: dependencies<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; command 1<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; command 2<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;...<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; command n<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal">其中，<span lang="EN-US">target</span>是我们构建<span lang="EN-US">(Build)</span>的目标，而<span lang="EN-US">dependencies</span>是构建该目标所需的其它文件或其他目标。之后是构建出该目标所需执行的指令。 有一点尤为需要注意：每一个指令<span lang="EN-US">(command)</span>之前必须有一个<span lang="EN-US">TAB</span>。这里必须使用<span lang="EN-US">TAB</span>而不能是空格，否则<span lang="EN-US">make</span>会报错。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal">我们的简易的<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>可以写成如下的样子，之后执行<span lang="EN-US">make</span>即可产生<span lang="EN-US">hello_world</span>这个可执行文件。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">all: hello_world.c<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; gcc -o hello_world hello_world.c<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p><span style="font-size: 10.5pt; font-family: 'Open Sans', Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">理解了<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>最基本的概念后，我们来看一下我们的小操作系统的最顶层的<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>。由于<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>是用于指导程序如何被构建的， 因此，通过阅读<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>，我们就可以理解源代码被构建成可执行文件的过程。这一过程可以给我们一些阅读代码的提示， 可以说，<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>就像源代码的地图，告诉你源代码是如何一步一步成为最终的可执行文件的。下面的代码是实验代码最顶层的<span lang="EN-US">Makefile</span>， 通过阅读它我们就能了解代码中很多宏观的东西。文本内容详见lab1章节Let's hack the kernel!</span></p> </div> </div> <div class="vert vert-1"
